posted:Posted June 3, 2024
msg:When traveling with children to Jinan, InterContinental is still the first choice. The excellent geographical location and the comfortable and comfortable stay experience complement the beautiful scenery and food of the Spring City.
In terms of guest service, I received a call from Xiaohua as soon as I got off the high-speed rail, and he took the initiative to upgrade us to a children's theme room facing Daming Lake. After checking out, I called again to ask about the experience.
In terms of catering, I originally wanted to take my children to experience the special breakfast, but the hotel's buffet breakfast not only had braised meat, beef soup, and sweet foam, but also the buns were freshly made. The Chinese store and Western pastries are all in good shape, and the pancakes and cakes are delicious. It is particularly worth mentioning that the bacon is crispy, which is a big surprise. Wendy meng in the restaurant is very considerate and asked if I needed to bring some milk snacks for the children to eat while playing. This is an experience I have never had before.
Because I planned to take a cruise to Heihu Spring, I applied to the front desk for a delayed check-out. Before I said the time, the switchboard Xiao Yang took the initiative to delay it for us until 4 pm. Let us pack up our things safely after playing, take a rest and go to the station.
In short, the service of Luneng Guihe InterContinental is absolutely above the standard, and it is no exaggeration to say that it is the world's leading.
The only suggestion: put tissue paper on the washbasin.
Everything else is perfect and dreamy, looking forward to staying next time!

The five-star standard is beyond words. It is very warm and warm. Comfortable.

Room:
The overall flow is smooth, from the entrance to the dressing room to the bathroom to the bed area to the sofa area to the floor-to-ceiling windows. The straight line is very spacious, the carpet is very soft and quiet, and the swivel chair is a bit hard.

Supporting hardware:
The TV is a bit old and only has common satellite channels. I really recommend Internet TV. Everything else is OK.
The bathroom fixtures are obviously Kohler, and the exhaust effect is average. The same-channel sound amplification in the bathroom is a definite plus. You can watch the TV in the room through the partition glass while taking a bath.

Parent-child room layout:
In the parent-child room booked this time, most of the corners of the furniture were protected with anti-collision corner guards. However, it was obviously not a professional parent-child room. It was only remodeled later because all the furniture was not rounded and there were still many corners. The risk of injury, especially with small slides, is even more dangerous, and it is recommended to do more risk management.
This time it was for the small tent and the small slide, because the child had just learned to walk at 15 months old, and the small slide was very new, which was a plus. I like the small tent very much at night. I hug a stuffed bear and am very happy. It is recommended that the stuffed bears placed in the tent can be given away with the guests, or canceled, because they are very cute to the little ones, but it is really cruel to let them go after leaving. The furry bear is very soft.

Meals:
I only had breakfast at the hotel, leaving the rest for next time. The breakfast alone is very good, but it can only be eaten in dine-in, and the room delivery service can only be done after 10:30. I may have to wait until the end of the dine-in breakfast. I hope it can be done. At the same time.
The dishes are pretty good, very rich, with a complete mix of meat and vegetables, a lot of hot and cold combinations, and a perfect combination of Chinese and Western. You still have to be careful not to take too many dishes at the buffet, because you can really last it. Seeing your baby eating happily proves everything. , very good breakfast restaurant.

Shopping and entertainment:
It is a shopping mall in itself, similar to SKP. It is very convenient to buy bags and shoes. LV styles are average. Gucci is a little later but can make up for it. Dior escaped without paying attention.
Next to it are two relatively large shopping plazas, which are very lively during the day and night. They can also meet your shopping needs at any time during vacation, which is perfect.

Attractions nearby:
Close to Daming Lake, 15 minutes' walk. Baotu Spring, 10 minutes walk. Black Tiger Spring, 10 minutes walk. They are all within walking distance, suitable for all ages. It is very comfortable to have something to eat and visit the sights.

Travel:
The transportation is very convenient, and the scenic spots are within walking distance. Because it seems difficult to park at the scenic spots, we all walked with a stroller. Shandong people's drivers are very friendly to pedestrians and will give way to places where there are no traffic lights.

Generally speaking, my trip to Jinan has been very beautiful since I checked into the hotel. I will definitely come back next time. Thank you to all the staff.

The hotel is located near Daming Lake, and it is not far from Daming Lake, Baotu Spring, Black Tiger Spring and Furong Street. The surrounding business is very prosperous, shopping and eating are very convenient.
Transportation: It is a relatively central location in the old city, but there will be traffic jams when taking a taxi. Fortunately, the places to eat, drink and play are relatively close. It is recommended to walk.
Hygiene: The overall hygiene is good. After all, it is an old hotel, and there are still some traces of time. The service auntie is more serious about cleaning, and the service is also good. However, the details still need to be improved. For example, some fluffy dust can be seen in the ceiling light trough, and the stains on the edge of the bathroom sink have not been cleaned.
Environment: The environment of the hotel is relatively good. Personally, I like the zigzag corridor, the bright ceiling, bright during the day and warm at night, which makes people feel very comfortable. The swimming pool looks good, but unfortunately I forgot to bring a swimsuit, and the time for the three-day tour was relatively rushed, so I didn't go to experience it. The breakfast is also the best among the five-star hotel buffets I have eaten recently. There are many choices and fresh ingredients.
Service: Shandong people are very warm, the overall service is very good, the aunt in the room, the restaurant, and the front desk are all very good. It is worth mentioning that the service of the switchboard Xiao Yang is excellent, with five-star praise.

In general, it is a good choice to stay at Intercontinental for personal travel, it is worth recommendingüëçüèª
